  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8c0b74f7-da0b-4505-a207-17b8466b7f11'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText11063215585652830748" style="display:none"><b>#1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author Ilona Andrews launches a brand new Hidden Legacy series, in which one woman must place her trust in a seductive, dangerous man who sets off an even more dangerous desire…</b><br /><br />Nevada Baylor is faced with the most challenging case of her detective career—a suicide mission to bring in a suspect in a volatile case. Nevada isn't sure she has the chops. Her quarry is a Prime, the highest rank of magic user, who can set anyone and anything on fire.<br /><br />Then she's kidnapped by Connor "Mad" Rogan—a darkly tempting billionaire with equally devastating powers. Torn between wanting to run or surrender to their overwhelming attraction, Nevada must join forces with Rogan to stay alive.<br /><br />Rogan's after the same target, so he needs Nevada. But she's getting under his skin, making him care about someone other than himself for a change. And, as Rogan has learned, love can be as perilous as death, especially in the magic world.</span>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/171624-okay-i-m-a-bit-worried-by-the-cover-i">Okay. I&#39;m a bit worried by the cover. I have read most of everything the Andrews team has written, but I&#39;m not really into PR. Is this more graphic than past novels? The Kate Daniels series tops it for me in terms of swearing and the The Edge series tops it for me in terms of bedroom scenes (or shed scenes, or whatever). Where does this book fit in on the I&#39;m-a-prude scale?</a>
</div>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/29827048-briar">Briar</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The cover did not do this book justice and I suspect the person who chose the cover didn't actually read the book. They probably heard words "heroine,<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The cover did not do this book justice and I suspect the person who chose the cover didn't actually read the book. They probably heard words "heroine," "hero," "Burn for Me" and decided to make a cheesy PR cover. However, let me be clear. I would not classify this as PR. This is an epic urban-fantasy series that I can not wait to see more of.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_866512435" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/866512435" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/866512435?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20799724-burn-for-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=rabid-reads-reviews">rabid-reads-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=jerk-of-my-dreams">jerk-of-my-dreams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=some-kinda-magic">some-kinda-magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=superheroes-superhero-like-powers">superheroes-superhero-like-powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=edelweiss">edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer866512435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9892848473065571926"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2014/10/early-review-burn-for-me-by-ilona-andrews.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a></b><br/><br/>For those of you who <s>have been living under a rock</s> don’t already know, Ilona Andrews is my F-A-V-O-R-I-T-E.<br/><br/>Has been since I first read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_' title='Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Magic Bites</a> five or six years ago. After I binge-read all the available Kate books, I moved onto <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/46801-the-edge' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Edge</a>
</b> which I also loved, and knowing that the Ilona love was <i>not</i> a fluke, the internet stalking began, in which I discovered the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20295040.Curran_POV_Collection' title='Curran POV Collection by Gordon Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Curran POV Collection</a> and <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/66326-kinsmen' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kinsmen</a>
</b> sci-fi short stories, etc.<br/><br/>And the Andrews, have never, not once, let </span>
  <span id="freeText9892848473065571926" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2014/10/early-review-burn-for-me-by-ilona-andrews.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a></b><br><br>For those of you who <s>have been living under a rock</s> don’t already know, Ilona Andrews is my F-A-V-O-R-I-T-E.<br><br>Has been since I first read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_" title="Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> five or six years ago. After I binge-read all the available Kate books, I moved onto <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/46801-the-edge" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge</a>
</b> which I also loved, and knowing that the Ilona love was <i>not</i> a fluke, the internet stalking began, in which I discovered the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20295040.Curran_POV_Collection" title="Curran POV Collection by Gordon Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Curran POV Collection</a> and <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/66326-kinsmen" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Kinsmen</a>
</b> sci-fi short stories, etc.<br><br>And the Andrews, have never, not once, let me down.<br><br>BURN FOR ME, the first installment of the HIDDEN LEGACY series, takes place in a world where a few hundred years ago a serum was discovered that could awaken a myriad of different types of magic in humans. Eventually the serum was destroyed, but the damage had already been done, and the newly awakened magical gifts were passed on genetically. Fast forward to the present, and the highly magical families guard their bloodlines the same way the real world Western European blue bloods do.<br><br>Enter Nevada Baylor, who at 25 has had the responsibility of keeping the family PI business afloat since her father died of cancer six years ago.<br><br>The family PI business whose mortgage was sold to one of the Big Deal magical families in order to pay the medical bills. The family PI business the Big Deal magical family is offering up as a sacrificial lamb when our story begins.<br><br>Baylor Investigative Agency looks great on paper, you see, and Montgomery International Investigations (MII) has been asked by another Big Deal magical family to bring in their prodigal son, a Prime (the highest level of magic user) pyro(FIRE)kinetic, who just recently burnt up a bank, which resulted in the death of a cop amongst other things. MII, being unable to refuse such a request without risking unpleasantness, weighed the risks, deemed an honest attempt too expensive, and decided to make use of the clause in the mortgage agreement that allows them to contract out Nevada’s services.<br><br>If she refuses, she breaks the contract, and the business is forfeit. If she fails, she breaks the contract, and the business is forfeit. If she <i>dies</i>, MII gets to recoup their loses, and the business is forfeit.<br><br>And this was the point where I shrieked my vicarious RAGE and scared the crap out of my cat. Seriously. He sat on the floor in front of the bed for the rest of the day. Wouldn’t come near me . . .<br><br>Such was the level of emotion the book was able to pull out of me, and that was in the first 8%.<br><br>That’s one of my favorite things about the Andrews—their ability to create instantly likable and/or interesting characters. Slews of them. Nevada is a perfect example of this. She’s snarky and fantastic, so much so that you don’t mind or begrudge her her super special snowflake status.<br><br>Nevada’s family is the “slew,” her grandmother <i>especially</i> is a hoot, and then there’s Mad Rogan . . .<br><br>Mad Rogan, a Prime with off-the-charts magical abilities . . . Mad Rogan, the wealthy and powerful head of House Rogan . . . Mad Rogan, pure sex walking around on two legs . . .<br><br>Mad Rogan, the borderline sociopath.<br><br>Yes, you heard me: SOCIOPATH.<br><br>I can only hope more is revealed in future installments to make him a more sympathetic character, b/c, right now, Mad Rogan is my only real issue with this book.<br><br>Oh, there was also some slight disbelief with the Big Reveal at the very end, but that was small potatoes. Mad Rogan, on the other hand . . . he’s downright scary. Like Ted Bundy scary. And I can see Nevada being hot for him, but eventually in <i>love</i> with him . . . ? As it stands, she should run screaming, in the opposite direction.<br><br>Literally Mad Rogan aside, <i>Burn for Me</i> is positively delightful. The world-building is fresh and original. The characters are hilarious, and the sense of family will give you the warm-fuzzies. Those of you who <s>stalk</s> follow the Andrews like I do will particularly enjoy a scenario with Nevada’s high school-aged sisters that very closely resembled something that happened with one of their daughters—the pen is mightier than the high school coach. *wink* Overall, an excellent start to a wonderful new series. Nevada Baylor is now second to only Kate Daniels. Highly recommended.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393496825ra/8722628.gif" width="300" height="169" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And if you're interested, you can find my interview with the Andrews about this book <b>
  <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2014/11/interview-with-ilona-andrews-author-of-burn-for-me.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>
</b>.<br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088286483" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot (Hidden Legacy, #2)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434251816" rel="nofollow noopener">Wildfire (Hidden Legacy, #3)</a>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9892848473065571926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084926558" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17958962380818030893">➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rerererererererererereread is</u>
</b>: I don't understand why everyone is so desperately looking for a <b>covid-19 vaccine</b> right now, when they could just call The Butcher of Merida for help. I mean, I'm pretty sure Rogan would <b>make the pesky virus go "splat!" Peaches-style</b> in less time than it takes to say "unleash the murderous crustaceans" and stuff.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601200945ra/30159574.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>I have the best ideas, I know.</i><br/><br/>👋 Until next time and stuff.<br/><br/>· <b>Book 2</b>: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094380151' rel='nofollow noopener'>White Hot</a> ★★★★★<br/>· <b>Book 3</b>: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1502577081' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wildfire</a> ★★★★★<br/>· <b>Book 3.5</b>: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2351162859' rel='nofollow noopener'>Diamond F</a></span>
  <span id="freeText17958962380818030893" style="display:none">➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rerererererererererereread is</u>
</b>: I don't understand why everyone is so desperately looking for a <b>covid-19 vaccine</b> right now, when they could just call The Butcher of Merida for help. I mean, I'm pretty sure Rogan would <b>make the pesky virus go "splat!" Peaches-style</b> in less time than it takes to say "unleash the murderous crustaceans" and stuff.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601200945ra/30159574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>I have the best ideas, I know.</i><br><br>👋 Until next time and stuff.<br><br>· <b>Book 2</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094380151" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 3</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1502577081" rel="nofollow noopener">Wildfire</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 3.5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2351162859" rel="nofollow noopener">Diamond Fire</a> ★★★<br>· <b>Book 4</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2371214665" rel="nofollow noopener">Sapphire Flames</a> ★★★<br>· <b>Book 5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2371214840" rel="nofollow noopener">Emerald Blaze</a> - <i>to be read</i><br>· <b>Book 6</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2371215027" rel="nofollow noopener">Ruby Fever</a> - <i>to be released</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>March 13, 2019</b>]<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rererererererererereread is</u>
</b>: it is a truth universally acknowledged that <s>the Scourge of Mexico</s> this book is <b>the ultimate cure for <s>all book slumps</s> everything</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552550236ra/27201791.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>👋 Until next time and stuff.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>May 2, 2018</b>]<br><br>💉 <b>Some Clueless People Use Illegal Drugs to Get High But That's Just Because They're Um Clueless and Stuff and Have Never Read a <s>Tactile</s> IA Book Before Ha Buddy Rerererererererereread</b> (SCPUIDtGHBTJBTUCaSaHNRa<s>T</s>IABBHBR™) with the IA Addicts 💉<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rerererererereread is</u>
</b>: can I beat the crap out of Adam Pierce? <b>Please</b>? Pretty please? I promise to be nice and behave and <b>not skewer puny humans</b> for at least a day and stuff! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552252361ra/27186283.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S.</b> I really don't understand why <b>antidepressants</b> are still being prescribed when this series is readily available. Doctors are <b>really weird</b>, if you ask me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>May 28, 2017</b>]<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rerererererereread is</u>
</b>:<br><br>Sorry, what? I only just rerererererereread this a month ago, you say? And your point is?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552252361ra/27186284.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S.</b> I want to be Nevada Baylor when I grow up. And not only because the Scourge of Mexico wants to go all tactile on <s>me</s> her and stuff. Not that I mind the Scourge of Mexico wanting to go all tactile on <s>me</s> her and stuff. But, you know, there's other, you know, cool stuff about being her that makes me want to, you know, be her and stuff.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>April 22, 2017</b>]<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rererererereread is</u>
</b>:<br><br>Weeeeeeeeeee!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492931004ra/22567717.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❣ <b>Real Life Sucks Too Much We Gotta Get Ourselves Some Tactile Now Poof All Problems Gone Impromptu Buddy Rerererererererereread</b> (RLSTMWGGOSTNPAPGIBR™) with the IA Addicts ❣<br><br>➽ <u>And the moralsssss of this rerererererereread are</u>:<br><br>① <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429708107ra/14622719.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>② <b>I want to be Nevada Baylor when I grow up</b>. Because <s>Mad Rogan</s> reasons.<br><br>③ <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480002628i/21262745.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>④ <b>The cow didn't do it</b>.<br><br>⑤ <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480004499i/21263029.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>No idea what DNA helicase is? Me neither. Who the shrimp cares, anyway? You get the idea, right? Right. So?</i><br><br>⑥ <b>Best IA banter and dialogues</b> in the history of IA banter and dialogues.<br><br>⑦ <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474544280ra/20613533.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑧ Best <b>car wrecking extravaganza</b> in the history of car wrecking extravaganzas.<br><br>⑨ <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480004857i/21263079._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑩ <b>Exposure therapy</b> is all about <b>snake handling</b>.<br><br>⑪ <b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480004715ra/21263074.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑫ TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. <b>Obviously</b>.<br><br>» <b>And the moral of the moralsssss of this crappy non review is</b>: I might be slightly obsessed with Mad Rogan. Not sure. The jury's still out on that one.<br><br><b>Bye now</b>. Until next time. You're welcome. And stuff.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>Mad Rogan</b>=<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480003481ra/21262852.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>No, I am not obsessed. Absolutely not.</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>October 2015 rerereread</b>]<br><br><b>Previous rating</b>: 8 stars.<br><b>New rating</b>: 10 stars.<br><br>✔ <b>YES</b> I have read this book FOUR times in less than a year.<br>✘ <b>NO</b> it's not particularly deep.<br>✘ <b>NO</b> it's not particularly philosophical.<br><br>►► <b>BUT</b> ◄◄<br><br>✔ <b>YES</b> it's bloody entertaining.<br>✔ <b>YES</b> it features high-quality, hilarious IA banter.<br>✔ <b>YES</b> I love ALL the characters. YES, every single one of them.<br>✔ <b>YES</b> it's the best alternative to anti-depressants I've ever come across. <br><br>❂❂ <b>Ilona, Gordon, you're my life savers</b> ❂❂<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423385286i/13617639.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❣ Buddy rerereread with the <s>eye candy</s> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">IA</a> addicts starting April 20, 2015 ❣<br><br><b>This is the third time</b> I read this book in the last six months. Were you expecting a full-length review? <b>Too bad</b>.<br><br><i>☆☆☆ Book Covers From Hell Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Burn For Me: A Crash Course</b><br><br>① <b>Nevada Baylor</b>: I love you. Because buzzer magic. And because no matter how infuriatingly hot IA's male leads are, the damsel in <s>distress</s> residence always kicks ass and saves the day.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429887657i/14640508.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>② <b>Mad Rogan aka The Scourge of Mexico:</b> MINE. Because hottest mass murderer ever. And because TACTILE. Need I say more? <b>Didn't think so</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429887657i/14640509._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>③ <b>Grandma Frida</b>: coolest grandma ever. Because mech mage and military vet. Because armoured vehicles and tanks. And because weakness for shirtless hunks. <b>I want to adopt you</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429888247i/14640539.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>→ yes, I know this gif has nothing to do with this story. And your point is? I never said any of this was supposed to make sense.</i><br><br>④ <b>Secondary character heaven</b>: sniper mom ✔ Pancakes ✔ Ever shirtless Adam Pierce ✔ Dysfunctional cousins ✔ Addicted Bug ✔ Exasperating teenage sisters ✔ O’Leary's cow ✔ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797575i/633609.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑤ <b>Chopsticks</b>. Everything kinetic. Flying greyhound busses. Levitating in parks. Shaking buildings. Exploding buildings. Rearranged buildings. Sliced up buildings ← yes, this book is a <b>builder's dream</b>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429891974i/14640893._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>⑥ <b>You know there's something missing</b> here don't you? Don't tell me you didn't notice. I've barely mentioned it so far. And it's my #1 obsession. Still don't know what I'm talking about? I'll keep short and simple: <b>TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429891974i/14640894.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✎ <b>Added bonus</b>: the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22303684-white-hot?from_search=true&amp;search_exp_group=group_a&amp;search_version=service" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot</a> Cover From Hell mystery is now solved. The publishers got their male character wrong. They thought book 2 would be <b>about Adam Pierce</b> and his "terminal fear of T-shirts or any other garment that would cover his pectorals." Ha! I've got two words for you Dear Publishers: <b>MAD ROGAN</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE. TACTILE <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>Simple maths time again</u>
</b>:<br><br>IA <b>greatness <br>-</b><br>Book cover from <b>hell <br>-</b><br><b>Tacky</b> title<b><br>=</b><br><b>I'm raising my rating to 8 stars</b>. QED and stuff.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446675500i/16864265.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>First re-read: December 2014</b>]<br><br><b>Original rating: 4<br>New rating: 5</b><br><br><b>This book? Too awesome for words.</b> So awesome I could start re-reading it again right away. So awesome I don't even feel like reviewing it again. <br><br><b>I think I'll just stick to a list of random awesomeness:</b><br>The Osiris serum. <b>Nevada.</b> United Native Tribes. <b>The Butcher of Merida.</b> Sniper mom. <b>Hilarious dialogues.</b> The chopsticks scene. Armored cars. <b>Grandma Frida.</b> Mexico, the magical juggernaut. Grandma Frida hanging up on Mad Rogan. <b>Huracan.</b> Swarmers. Snifers. <b>Truthseekers.</b> Carnations. Pyrokinetics. <b>Squirrels.</b> Augustine "Pancakes" Montgomery. The dinner conversation between Rogan &amp; Leon. <b>The Scourge of Mexico.</b> Time stopping and fast forwarding. <b>Tactile.</b> The Key. Rogan shaking the warehouse. <b>Shockers.</b> Wind mages. Breakers. Aquakinetics. <b>The Bridge Park scene. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400567ra/776499.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>Original review (Oct 2014)</b>]<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/2063921-clean-sweep" rel="nofollow noopener">Group read</a> with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">IAA</a> bunch.</b><br><br><b>Let’s get two things out of the way real quick:</b> <br><br><b>First, the book cover.</b> I cannot even begin to comprehend what happened there. What publisher in their right mind would choose such a trashy-romance-looking cover for a UF book by Ilona Andrews? I just don’t get it. [ETA: it turns out the Andrews had chosen an <a href="http://www.ilona-andrews.com/blog/2014/11/03/secret-secrets/" rel="nofollow noopener">alternate cover</a> for this book but several retailers thought it wouldn't sell {insert major eye roll here} so they went for this one instead.] <br><br><b>Second, the inevitable Kate Daniels comparison.</b> I have to admit I had KD in mind when I started reading Burn for Me but quickly decided to stop comparing the books and just enjoy what I was reading. Burn for Me is a great introduction to the Hidden Legacy series but it is a much lighter read than KD. Granted, as it is the first instalment in a new series, the world building will probably expand and become more complex, which I am really looking forward to.<br><br><b>So, back to Burn for Me.</b> This book was so much FUN to read! I really enjoyed the premise of the book: a serum that revealed different types of magic inherent to humans about a hundred years ago, the destruction of said serum and then the use of genetics to pass the magic from one generation to another. <b>Highly magical (and very wealthy) families</b> are prepared to go to great lengths to keep their bloodlines intact and increase their magic. Now that’s one fantastic premise! The world building is great and I love the mix of magic with the military, heavy weaponry, armored everything… It makes for a very original world.<br><br><b>Then we have our heroine, Nevada Baylor,</b> who has been running the family PI business since her father died. I don’t want to go into much detail here but as the story begins the business is on shaky ground and Nevada is doing her best to keep the family afloat. <b>Nevada is a fantastic character,</b> she is straightforward, principled and snarky as hell. I loved her from the very beginning. She lives in a huge warehouse with her hilarious grandmother, her mother, her two teenage sisters and her two cousins. They all contribute to the business in their own way and make a great family. I really enjoyed their interactions.<br><br><b>Now for Mad Rogan, our mass murderer hero.</b> I mean, just how cool is that? A mass murderer/sociopath hero?! Only the Andrews I tell you! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[To be honest, Rogan might be ruthless but after having read the book he doesn’t seem to be much of a sociopath. He was in the army and killed lots of people during the war, does that mean he qualifies as a mass murderer? I don’t know. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So. The guy is sizzling hot. Sorry, I meant <b>sizzling hot</b>. There are a couple of scenes there <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(first when he shows Nevada what it means to be a –hum– Tactile then the whole scene that leads to their first kiss and…) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that had me swooning, sighing &amp; panting. <b>The works.</b> I can't imagine what will happen the day these two go beyond the kissing stage^^ *rubs hands in anticipation* One thing that did bother me about Rogan: the never-ending descriptions of how hot and sexy he is. Amazing abs, great chest, broad shoulders, strong biceps, incredible eyes… I got it the first three times, no need to re-hash it over and over again. But that’s a minor quibble really.<br><br><b>Put Nevada and Rogan together, shake well</b> and you get great chemistry and fantastic banter. So many great lines there, I wish I could quote them all but there wouldn’t be enough space in this review so I’ll just pick three:<br><blockquote>“<b>And let’s be honest</b>, you weren’t exactly harmed. I even took you home.” “You dumped me on my doorstep. According to my mother, I looked <b>half dead</b>.” “Your mother exaggerates. A third dead at most.” I stared at him. <b>Wow. Just wow.</b>
</blockquote><blockquote>“<b>Why can’t you just</b> slice them to pieces like that chopstick?” “Because my telekinetic magic doesn’t work on living things.” [...] Oh. “So the best way to fight you is to <b>strip naked and attack</b>?” His eyes flashed with a wicked light. “Yes. You should try it and see what happens.” Well, <b>I did walk right into that one</b>.</blockquote><blockquote>“<b>Mr Rogan</b>,” I frosted my voice over. “What I put into my body is my business.” Okay, <b>that didn’t sound right</b>.</blockquote><b>Burn for Me has it all:</b> action, suspense, lots of magic, great characterization, world building with lots of potential and sizzling hot chemistry between the two main characters. I’m definitely planning to be read it again before its sequel comes out in 2015!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">THE ENTIRE WORLD or at least those who like UF without Vampires.</span></div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9448912139876059263"><b>Re-read of the series in May and June</b><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520192269i/25161626.jpg' width='400' height='218' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>5th read and I still love practically everything about this book. It is like coming home after a long trip away and just being so happy to be there again. If you haven't started this series yet you are missing out in my honest and very humble yet biased opinion <br/><br/><b>Rereading Again....for no reason what-so-ever</b> *whistles nonchalantly*<br/><br/><b>Buddy Read with <a href='%E2%80%9D' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alexa</a>, <a>Athena</a>, <a>Ya</a>, <a>Carole</a>, <a>oOSarahOo</a>, and <a>Sandra</a></b><br/><br/>Fantastic and fun buddy read with some great girls. Totally wort</span>
  <span id="freeText9448912139876059263" style="display:none"><b>Re-read of the series in May and June</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520192269i/25161626.jpg" width="400" height="218" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>5th read and I still love practically everything about this book. It is like coming home after a long trip away and just being so happy to be there again. If you haven't started this series yet you are missing out in my honest and very humble yet biased opinion <br><br><b>Rereading Again....for no reason what-so-ever</b> *whistles nonchalantly*<br><br><b>Buddy Read with <a href="%E2%80%9D" rel="nofollow noopener">Alexa</a>, <a>Athena</a>, <a>Ya</a>, <a>Carole</a>, <a>oOSarahOo</a>, and <a>Sandra</a></b><br><br>Fantastic and fun buddy read with some great girls. Totally worth the re-read less than a month later <br><br>Kindle highlight count 149 (I might have a problem)<br><br><b>LOVED IT, Loved it, LOVED IT!!! </b> 4-4.5 Mad Rogan Stars.<br><br>Spoiler Free Review - <br><br><b>Top 5 Reasons I Love anything Ilona Andrews:</b><br><br>1.	 Fan-Freaking-Tastic build-up of sexual tension.<br>2.	 Never disappoint in making entirely new worlds and new magic systems.<br>3.	 They know how to make interesting side characters that add to the story.<br>4.	 Blending humor with action and suspense<br>5.	 I want to live in these worlds. I want to hang out in Nevada’s warehouse home and play on Herald. Or hang with Kate at the Keep, go with Andrea to the shooting range and drink some of Doolittle’s Honeybadger tea. I’d love to go on an adventure with George, Jack and Sophie and I need to visit Dina’s Inn and play with her broom. I read all of their books over and over and love them more every time. <br><br>Simply put they are the best. How many authors can switch up their worlds and make each one just as interesting if not more interesting than the last? I can only name a few.<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/best_zps254aa930.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405632306ra/10428053.gif" alt=" photo best_zps254aa930.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Burn For Me has everything that I have come to expect and need from an Ilona Andrews novel. There is the strong Heroine who is tough and likable, Nevada. The charismatic male lead Mad Rogan, who is handsome, rich, powerful, unconventional and a handful, possibly even a bit crazy, the jury is still out on that one. <br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/diagonal_zps98fedcf0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413235146i/11481939.jpg" alt=" photo diagonal_zps98fedcf0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The bad guy/s are just as interesting as everything else. They are never quite what you would expect and sometimes they can give the Hero a run for the money with their wit, charm and burning sexuality.<br><br>It all adds up to a great ride. I loved my introduction into this new world. It has new rules, a very different backstory than any of IA’s prior books and a whole new cast of characters. I’m sure I’m going to love all of them. Nevada’s family seems ripe with possibilities and I really liked the detective agency she is running with a few of her older and younger family members. They are a hoot and one of the strangest families I’ve read in a little while.<br><br>The premise of the world is that some people through scientific help generations ago developed abilities to control different elements or energies. Something like X-men-ish type powers, anything from talking to animals, controlling fire, telekinesis to working with metals or plants. It was deemed incredible dangerous and so the serum used was banned and now generations have gone by where some families have coalesced their power through breeding over generations to become the strongest they could possibly be. Mad Rogan is a byproduct and head of such a family.<br><br>Nevada’s family detective agency is owned by another powerful family and she has been commissioned to find one of its members before the police find him. Shouldn’t be too hard, except Adam is wanted for murder, extremely powerful and has an unusual fascination with Nevada.<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/psyco_zps18707739.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412303275ra/11355931.gif" alt=" photo psyco_zps18707739.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When Mad Rogan and Nevada’s paths meet in search of the same thing it doesn’t all go well.<br><br><b>
  <i>“So instead of talking to me, asking for my credentials, or doing any of those things a normal person would do, you decided to assault me and chain me in your basement?”<br>He shrugged a, slow, deliberate movement. “It seemed like the most expedient way to obtain the information. And let’s be honest, you weren’t exactly harmed. I even took you home.”<br>“You dumped me on my doorstep. According to my mother, I looked half dead.”<br>“Your mother exaggerates. A third dead at most.”</i>
</b><br><br>These two together really made the book for me. I ship them so hard. They are completely different and the way they rub against each other had me laughing and smiling just waiting for when something even hotter was going to happen. This is a slow building romance that I’m going to enjoy to build up for no matter how many books it takes…<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>“Fine,” he said. “You had no idea it could be this good. Nobody in your past was ever that good and you know that nobody in your future will ever be this good. You’ve had a taste and you want more. You want sex. Dirty, naked hot sex. It’s floating through your head as we speak. You think you can imagine what it would be like. Trust me, you have no idea. I haven’t even started. So run from it, think it over, pretend it didn’t happen, it doesn’t matter. I’ll allow it for now. The more you fight, the more irresistible it will become, until one day I’ll motion with my hand and you’ll come running.”</i>
  <br>
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><i>please in the next book…I love them please….</i> <br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/nopants_zps7e026a46.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413235146i/11481940.jpg" alt=" photo nopants_zps7e026a46.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> IA has this special way of making me love their characters. They aren’t perfect, they are scared or had deep seated issues of some kind hidden away, and I love ever new revelation and facet of them. I’m totally ready to dig in deeper and find out what makes Nevada and Mad Rogan especially tick.<br><br>Another winner from IA and I really can’t wait to read it again. Which is why I’m re-reading it with some GR buddies when it come out.<br><br>In Short….<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/Read_this_zps8706f1dc.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411041291i/11187078.png" alt=" photo Read_this_zps8706f1dc.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>p.s. I will post a few more quotes after the book come out.<br>p.p.s. Thank you to _______ for the ARC, you know who you are and I love you for sending your copy to me</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1135744538" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1135744538" />
    <a title="Navessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa"><img alt="Navessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444162983p2/18104163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1135744538?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Navessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Navessa" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa">Navessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=mc-you-can-root-for">mc-you-can-root-for</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1135744538" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1602510430314376917">Let's talk about expectations, shall we? A few years ago, I went on a business trip to London. I was good friends with the co-workers I traveled with, and already had a fantastic rapport going with our British counterparts because I served as the liaison between our two companies. <br/><br/>The trip was a roaring success; everyone not only got along, but got along <i>really</i> well, and because of this dynamic, we accomplished everything we set out to early on in the week. That left us with a lot of free time t</span>
  <span id="freeText1602510430314376917" style="display:none">Let's talk about expectations, shall we? A few years ago, I went on a business trip to London. I was good friends with the co-workers I traveled with, and already had a fantastic rapport going with our British counterparts because I served as the liaison between our two companies. <br><br>The trip was a roaring success; everyone not only got along, but got along <i>really</i> well, and because of this dynamic, we accomplished everything we set out to early on in the week. That left us with a lot of free time to tour the city. <br><br>And by tour the city, I mean tour the pubs.<br><br>Each night after work, we would pour forth from the office doors in search of the nearest or loudest watering hole. One evening, already half-smashed thanks to the deceptively strong cider I'd been downing (seriously, what the hell is in that stuff?), I ordered pie off the menu, because apparently I fancied the idea of descending into a sugar-induced coma. <br><br>The "dessert" arrived a few minutes later, carrying with it the smell of golden pie crust and roasting meat. In my inebriated state, I brushed off the unexpected seared-flesh scent, thinking that it must have emanated from something else on the tray the bartender carried. I stabbed at the pie and lifted a steaming spoonful to my mouth. <br><br>Maybe, if I hadn't been absorbed in the conversation taking place at my table, or if I hadn't been such a goddamn lightweight, I would have noticed that something was off. I would have realized that my spoon hadn't slid into the pie with the same ease I would expect from a fruit-filled delicacy. I would have caught sight of the chunks of carrots and peas that ascended to my lips. I would have seen the massive chunk of meat hanging off my spoon. <br><br>Alas, I didn't. <br><br>Did I mention I'm a vegetarian? No? Ah, well, now you might understand why after biting into the carcass of a dead animal when I expected a dead fruit I tore out of the room and vomited spectacularly onto the sidewalk, narrowly missing a group of pedestrians. <br><br>It was all anyone talked about for the rest of the week. And when we briefed our boss on the success of the trip after arriving back home, one of my co-workers, who is sadistically quick on his feet, snuck a picture of my humiliation into the slide show. <br><br><b>-____-</b><br><br>I'm sure you're wondering what the hell this story has to do with <i>Burn for Me</i>. Well, let me tell you. I went into this expecting a paranormal romance. I had recently finished reading a book that had made me think about a lot of things - too many things - and I wanted to turn my brain off for a few blissful hours. I wanted something light and fluffy and sexy. <br><br>And really, with a title as cheesy as <i>Burn for Me</i>, who could blame me for thinking that this would deliver? Also, have you seen this cover? It promises certain things. Let me demonstrate what went through my mind when I first saw it:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419083317i/12986128.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Imagine my surprise when instead of witty banter and half-veiled propositions I was met with nearly a hundred pages of (shoddy) world building. I spent the first thirty percent of this book regretting my decision to pick it up. I spent the next twenty percent trying to stifle my hope, lest I be disappointed. I spent the last fifty percent enjoying the hell out of myself but also having some SERIOUS misgivings about all the woman-on-woman hatred and the shitbag of a male lead. In short, the second half of the book did not make up for the first, just balanced my rating out a little. <br><br>This was not the fluff-filled dessert that I had expected. This was a goddamn meat pie. <br><br><b><a href="http://www.thealliterates.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thealliterates" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the_alliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1602510430314376917" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_956732131" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/956732131" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/956732131?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer956732131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18212653610780093824">I'm not one of those readers who swears a favorite author can do no wrong. I feel I have to say this because it seems like every time I pick up an Ilona Andrews book, I find myself fawning all over it, like a teenage girl with her first crush. BUT IT'S REAL LOVE. I SWEAR.<br/><br/>This book rocked my socks off as much as any Kate Daniels book ever has. And while the Andrews team has a unique voice that is unmistakable, this book is not Kate: Part 2. The world-building is fantastic and utterly different fr</span>
  <span id="freeText18212653610780093824" style="display:none">I'm not one of those readers who swears a favorite author can do no wrong. I feel I have to say this because it seems like every time I pick up an Ilona Andrews book, I find myself fawning all over it, like a teenage girl with her first crush. BUT IT'S REAL LOVE. I SWEAR.<br /><br />This book rocked my socks off as much as any Kate Daniels book ever has. And while the Andrews team has a unique voice that is unmistakable, this book is not Kate: Part 2. The world-building is fantastic and utterly different from the some of the tired UF/ PNR templates I find in so many books of these genres. I loved the heroine. I loved the hero. I loved the unpredictable progression of the plot. And I loved the foundation of a romance that promises to be spectacular. I'm going to stop gushing for a moment and tell you a little about the story.<br /><br />It takes place in world where the wealthy and powerful wield magic, and create influential dynasties surrounding their skills. One of the strongest members of one of the most powerful families has gone rogue and now small-time PI Nevada Baylor is tasked to bring him in unharmed. She doesn't want the job. It's way out of her league, but circumstances force her hand and before she knows it, she is tackling a job too big for even the police to take on.<br /><br />Mad Rogan is a force just as powerful as Nevada's target. Maybe even more so. Which is why she wants nothing to do with him. But he has his own reasons to want to capture Adam Pierce and he knows Nevada may actually be savvy enough to do it. He pushes his way into her investigation --and into her life-- sparking a mutual attraction she can't control and he doesn't want to. Their mission is dangerous, exciting, and completely captivating from beginning to end.<br /><br />Nevada is impossible not to like. She's devoted to her family. She loves them and she's kind of taken over the mantle as the person responsible for them all. I love how Andrews paints these characters. They feel so real. They have quirks and color that make you feel like you know them; you can see why they mean so much to Nev. <br /><br />I love how smart the heroine is. How she tries to be practical instead of reckless. How she is so vastly powerful but has absolutely no idea.<br /><br />Rogan is totally badass. He can level cities with a thought. He is every bit the dragon of Nev's musings. But he is also more than that. I feel like she can teach him so much about what it means to be human... what it means to feel. The sexual tension between these two is off the charts. Her reactions to him are so hot and every time they touch, I am glued to the page.<br /><br />So I mentioned the great characters, the phenomenal world-building, and the scorching sexual tension. But I also have to give a shout-out to the awesome pacing and funny, funny one liners. Right in the middle of a serious conversation or observation, we're treated to inside jokes on tortured heroes and snake-penis metaphors. I laughed out loud more than once.<br /><br />It's smart. It's engaging. And I wouldn't change a thing.<br /><br />Disclosure: I beta read for this book. But I already considered it an A-read on the first pass. And I swear, if I didn't like it, I would tell you.<br /><br /><i>*ARC provided by author for review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18212653610780093824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend">recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=witchy-woman">witchy-woman</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040589267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3636694736224709426">4.5 stars<br/><br/><i>
  <b>HIDEOUS COVER ALERT*!</b>
</i><br/>I refuse to blame Andrews for this ridonkulous looking cheese-fest, but I wish that whoever is in charge of this sort of thing at Avon would get a clue.<br/>This looks like the sort of thing I've come to expect from crappy PNR, not Urban Fantasy. This cover doesn't say <b>kick-ass story between these pages</b>, it says <b>Fabio<i>ish</i> romance inside</b>. <br/>Well, guess what?<br/>They don't have sex in this book.<br/>The folks who were hoping for a little *bow-chicka-wow-wow* (<i>thanks to the cover</i>) </span>
  <span id="freeText3636694736224709426" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br /><i>
  <b>HIDEOUS COVER ALERT*!</b>
</i><br />I refuse to blame Andrews for this ridonkulous looking cheese-fest, but I wish that whoever is in charge of this sort of thing at Avon would get a clue.<br />This looks like the sort of thing I've come to expect from crappy PNR, not Urban Fantasy. This cover doesn't say <b>kick-ass story between these pages</b>, it says <b>Fabio<i>ish</i> romance inside</b>. <br />Well, guess what?<br />They don't have sex in this book.<br />The folks who were hoping for a little *bow-chicka-wow-wow* (<i>thanks to the cover</i>) will be disappointed.<br />And the people who don't want mindless PNR (<i>not that there's anything wrong with that!</i>) are going to bypass this book altogether.<br />Even <i>I</i> put off reading it, and I'm a fan of Ilona Andrews...so I should know better.<br /><i>
  <b>That's the power of a BAD cover, people!</b>
</i><br /><br />Alrighty, enough bitching.<br />I picked up <b>Burn For Me</b> and gobbled it down in record time.<br />I loved Nevada and her entire wacky family. Especially Grandma!<br />Surprisingly, I loved Mad Rogan, too. I see some complaints about him, but I thought he was awesome. Sure, it seems like he's sort of a sociopath, but I have a feeling he's a bit more complicated than that. <br />Or maybe not.<br />Either way, I thought he was great!<br /><br />Magic (<i>thanks to a scientific breakthrough</i>) is now a hereditary quality that the more powerful magic users in the world view as a commodity. They marry for the power it brings their families, and those Houses rule cities and corporations. <br />Or something like that.<br />The world-building wasn't fully explored, but I'm hoping that we'll get a better glimpse of how everything works in the next book. There was definitely enough information to get to get started with, though.<br /><br />I'm feeling really lazy, and I want to go eat some soup <s>and pie</s>.<br />So instead of trying to review the plot, I'll just say that if you're a fan of Ilona Andrews stuff, you're going to like this.<br /><br /><b>Highly Recommended to fans of Kate Daniels, Mercy Thompson, etc..</b><br /><br />*<i>No points were deducted for the horrible cover...</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3636694736224709426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1056795778" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1056795778" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1056795778?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=insta-love-lust">insta-love-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=my-precious">my-precious</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1056795778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10345296502455570431"><b>*****5/3/2017*****<br/><br/>There is a Mad Rogan POV scene on IA's site!!!!!<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.ilona-andrews.com/rogan-pov-from-burn-for-me-part-one/'>http://www.ilona-andrews.com/rogan-po...</a><br/><br/>5 If I Could I Would Kidnap IA And Make Them Tell Me Stories Forever Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417110905i/12214515.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>There might(definitely) be untagged SPOILERS.</u>
</b><br/><br/><i>In 1863 European scientists discovered the Osiris serum, a concoction which brought out one’s magic talents. These talents were many and varied. Eventually the world realized the consequences of awakening godlike powers in ordinary people. The serum was locked away, but </i></span>
  <span id="freeText10345296502455570431" style="display:none"><b>*****5/3/2017*****<br><br>There is a Mad Rogan POV scene on IA's site!!!!!<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.ilona-andrews.com/rogan-pov-from-burn-for-me-part-one/">http://www.ilona-andrews.com/rogan-po...</a><br><br>5 If I Could I Would Kidnap IA And Make Them Tell Me Stories Forever Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417110905i/12214515.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>There might(definitely) be untagged SPOILERS.</u>
</b><br><br><i>In 1863 European scientists discovered the Osiris serum, a concoction which brought out one’s magic talents. These talents were many and varied. Eventually the world realized the consequences of awakening godlike powers in ordinary people. The serum was locked away, but it was too late. The magic talents passed on from parents to their children and changed the course of human history forever. Those who previously married for status, money, and power now married for magic, because strong magic would give them everything.<br><br>Now, a century and a half later, families with strong hereditary magic have evolved into dynasties. It is a world where the more magic you have, the more powerful, the wealthier, and the more prominent you are. Some magic talents are destructive. Some are subtle. But no magic user should be taken lightly</i><br><br>In a world where Magic is the currency that talks and the Houses(families with strong magic genes) rule the world, Nevada Baylor is a very small fish in a huge pond. She works as a PI and she loves it buts he also carries the responsibility for her family's wellfare on her shoulders since her father's death. When MII, the company who owns their mortgage, sends Nevada in a suicide mission to deliver a Prime(the most powerful magic users) pyrokinitic who doesn't want to be delivered, back to his family, she has two options. Deny the job and lose everything, the bussiness, the house, the cars and all their savings, fail the job and lose everything, or succeed and earn a considerable amount of money. At least her family will get the bussiness back if the worst happens. Reassuring? Not really.<br><br>So Nevada has to manage to talk Adam, a narcissistic psychopath who has taken a liking for her, to return to his family and as if that wasn't enough, Mad Rogan, a Prime telekinetic with off the charts power, is after Adam too and is willing to walk all over her to get there. The chances of survival don't seem in her favor.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417114614i/12217031.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say that will describe IA's brilliant minds? This is the first installment in a brand new series, a brand new universe and I wasn't bored for a minute. The world building and the story were so well-done that I felt like I knew the rules from the beginning. No struggling to understand, no slow parts that magic is explained in length. They let the story flow and gave you enough information to keep you from being confused but not enough to overwhelm you.<br><br>Nevada is a brilliant heroine. She has Kate Daniels' spirit and snark but she is more responsible, more logical and not quite as quick to jump in dangerous situations. Just like Kate though danger seems to be drawn to her whether she wants or not. I liked how relatable Nevada was with her everyday problems of keeping her family bussiness afloat and her not always being the biggest badass around town. She is also highly moral and surprisingly law abiding which is a nice change for an UF heroine. The fact that she has a magic talent that must be hidden if she doesn't want to end up forced to do a job she won't like only adds more to the story.<br><br>And then comes Mad Rogan. Mad Rogan is powerful, arrogant, completely lacking in empathy and thinks everyone is beneath him. He is by all accounts a sociopath and makes no excuses. He used to work for the military but has retired and at the moment he has zero purpose in his life until he is given a distraction in the faces of Adam Pierce and Nevada Baylor. He could level a town with his power and probably wouldn't feel much regret later, he kills with hard, cold logic just like he does everything else in life. In a world full of badasses he knows he is the most badass of them all.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You have no regard for human life,” I said. “You saved the city, but I don’t think you did it because you genuinely cared about all those people. I think you did it because Adam Pierce got under your skin. You hire desperate soldiers, but you don’t do it to save them either. You do it because they offer you unquestioning loyalty. You rescued your cousin, but you had been content to ignore the existence of that whole branch of your family. You don’t feel that rules apply to you. If you want it, you buy it. If you can’t buy it, you take it. You don’t seem to feel bad about things, and you offer gratitude only when you need to overcome some hurdle. I think you might be a psychopath.<br>“I can’t be with you, no matter how crazy you make me, because you have no empathy, Rogan. I’m not talking about magic. I’m talking about the human ability to sympathize.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417114614i/12217032.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417114614ra/12217033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Adding to the awesomeness of the book is the fact that despite Nevada's attraction to Rogan she doesn't jump in bed with him. There is insta-lust but they don't act on it so it doesn't count. This is something that IA always do well, they develop the relationship, give it time and space to mature and by the time they get there you know why, you can't deny that they belong together. As frustrating as the unsatisfied sexual tension is, the end result is definitely worth it.<br><br>Also the bad guy of the story is suficiently cruel and demented but he isn't the one pulling the strings so we see the foundation for a bigger story arc. I want the next book so badly. We'll see how this develops but I have every faith I will ove it.<br><br>The secondary characters... IA know how to do secondary characters. From the overprotective mother who never misses a shot, to the crazy grandmother who loves a good eye-candy and is always there for everyone, to the teenage troublemakers in the family, they are all special snowflakes, hilarious and full of awesome. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're Mad Rogan!" Leon burst out.<br>"Yes," Mad Rogan said, his voice calm.<br>"And you can break cities?"<br>"Yes."<br>"And you have all this money and magic?"<br>"Yes."<br>Where was Leon going with this?<br>My cousin blinked. "And you look . . . like that?"<br>Mad Rogan nodded. "Yes."<br>Leon's dark eyes went wide. He looked at Mad Rogan, then glanced back at himself. At fifteen, Leon weighed barely a hundred pounds. His arms and legs were like chopsticks.<br>"There is no justice in the world!" Leon announced.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you’re really hard up, I can introduce you to my grandmother. She’s a fan.” Adam blinked. “She doesn’t typically sleep with pretty young things, but she would make an exception in your case. You might even learn a trick or two.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Do you have a girlfriend?” Grandma Frida asked. I put my hand over my face. <br>“No,” Mad Rogan said. <br>“A boyfriend?” Grandma Frida asked. <br>“No.” <br>“What about . . .” <br>“No,” Mom and I said in unison. <br>“But you don’t even know what I wanted to ask!” <br>“No,” we said again together. <br>“Party poopers.” Grandma shrugged.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Coming to a close to my description of why IA is awesome... I'm looking forward to knowing exactly how powerful Nevada is and how her exposure will go down. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It is obvious she will turn out to be a Prime after Rogan's cryptical comment when she was ranting about all the Primes' problems.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>“You know what your problem is? ‘You’ as in Primes, in general?”<br>“I think you’re about to tell me.” Mad Rogan leaned forward with rapt attention.<br>“Your problem is that nobody ever tells you no. You think you can do whatever you want, enter wherever you want . . .[...]You play with people’s lives. When cops show up, you wave your hand and make them go away. Because you are Primes and the rest of us are, apparently, nothing.”<br>“Mhm,” he said. “The irony of this is so rich, it’s simply delicious.”<br>“I don’t see what’s so ironic about it.”<br>“I’d tell you, but it would ruin the fun.”</i></b></blockquote>
<br><br>Yeap... I can see it coming already. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>That's all for now. It's a mile long worship letter!:P<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/316068.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>***************************************<br><br><b>Re-read April 2015<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425930182i/13952058.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
